[32mOptions (basic):[0m

[32mlayer[0m (str, default: [3m[0m):        Set the decoding layer
[32mgamma[0m (flt, default: [3m1[0m):       Set the float gamma value when decoding
[32mapply_trc[0m (sint, default: [3m2[0m, minmax: 1-18): color transfer characteristics to apply to EXR linear input
	 * [33mbt709[0m: BT.709
	 * [33mgamma[0m: gamma
	 * [33mgamma22[0m: BT.470 M
	 * [33mgamma28[0m: BT.470 BG
	 * [33msmpte170m[0m: SMPTE 170 M
	 * [33msmpte240m[0m: SMPTE 240 M
	 * [33mlinear[0m: Linear

[32mOptions (basic):[0m

[32mtxt_page[0m (str, default: [3m*[0m):    list of teletext page numbers to decode, * is all
[32mtxt_chop_top[0m (sint, default: [3m1[0m, minmax: 0-1): discards the top teletext line
[32mtxt_format[0m (sint, default: [3m0[0m, minmax: 0-1): format of the subtitles (bitmap or text)
 - bitmap
 - text
[32mtxt_left[0m (sint, default: [3m0[0m, minmax: 0-65535): x offset of generated bitmaps
[32mtxt_top[0m (sint, default: [3m0[0m, minmax: 0-65535): y offset of generated bitmaps
[32mtxt_chop_spaces[0m (sint, default: [3m1[0m, minmax: 0-1): chops leading and trailing spaces from text
